## 12. Deep Strategy Analysis & Application Guide

Each strategy is analyzed across all 8 robustness dimensions with specific application guidance and risk warnings.

### #1. Moving Average Crossover (MA)

**Type**: Trend-Following  
**Composite Score**: 43 | **Verdict**: **STRONG**  
**Trading Frequency**: Low (few trades per year)

#### Strategy Logic

Uses two moving averages (fast/slow). Buy when fast crosses above slow; sell when fast crosses below.

**Parameters**: `fast_period, slow_period`

#### Performance Summary

| Metric | Value | Interpretation |
|:---|:---:|:---|
| Walk-Forward Efficiency | +15.8% | Positive OOS returns |
| Generalization Gap | 45.4% | High overfitting risk |
| Param Stability | 0.662 | Moderate sensitivity |
| MC Robustness | 0.909 | Robust to price noise |
| OHLC Shuffle | 0.715 | Genuine price structure edge |
| Block Bootstrap | 0.016 | Sequence-dependent |
| Deflated Sharpe | 0.000 | High data-mining risk |
| Cross-Asset | +2453.6% | Generalizes across assets |

#### Best & Worst Assets

- **Best**: AVAX (+48.9%), MSTR (+37.1%), SOL (+35.5%), XRP (+20.6%), BTC (+20.2%)

#### Recommended Parameters (Top Assets)

| Asset | Optimal Params | Train | Val | Test | Stability |
|:---|:---|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| AVAX | (3, 11) | +11405.7% | -12.8% | -50.3% | 0.570 |
| MSTR | (3, 11) | +3818.3% | -14.8% | -24.0% | 0.753 |
| SOL | (9, 50) | +158474.8% | +3.0% | -27.3% | 0.764 |
| XRP | (3, 8) | +1261.2% | -37.0% | -22.7% | 0.446 |
| BTC | (31, 36) | +2280.1% | +0.7% | -28.5% | 0.262 |

#### Application Guide

- **Best suited for**: Strong trending markets with low noise
- **Key risk**: Whipsaws in sideways markets; lagging entries/exits
- **Recommendation**: Suitable for live deployment with proper risk management. Use the recommended parameters and monitor for regime changes.
- **Position sizing**: Start with 1-2% risk per trade. Scale up only after confirming live performance matches backtest expectations.

### #4. Relative Strength Index (RSI)

**Type**: Mean-Reversion  
**Composite Score**: 66 | **Verdict**: **MODERATE**  
**Trading Frequency**: Medium

#### Strategy Logic

Buy when RSI drops below oversold threshold; sell when RSI rises above overbought threshold.

**Parameters**: `rsi_period, oversold_threshold, overbought_threshold`

#### Performance Summary

| Metric | Value | Interpretation |
|:---|:---:|:---|
| Walk-Forward Efficiency | +8.3% | Positive OOS returns |
| Generalization Gap | 22.2% | High overfitting risk |
| Param Stability | 0.410 | Moderate sensitivity |
| MC Robustness | 0.808 | Robust to price noise |
| OHLC Shuffle | 0.376 | Genuine price structure edge |
| Block Bootstrap | 0.062 | Sequence-dependent |
| Deflated Sharpe | 0.056 | High data-mining risk |

## 14. Methodology

### 10-Layer Anti-Overfitting Pipeline

| Layer | Name | Purpose |
|:---:|:---|:---|
| 1 | Purged Walk-Forward | Train on historical, validate and test on future. Embargo gap prevents leakage. |
| 2 | Multi-Metric Scoring | Composite score: return / max_drawdown * trade_count_factor. |
| 3 | Minimum Trade Filter | Require >= 20 trades for statistical significance. |
| 4 | Parameter Stability | Perturb all params by +/-10% and +/-20%. Stable strategies survive. |
| 5 | Cross-Asset Validation | Test parameters trained on one asset across all other assets. |
| 6 | Monte Carlo Perturbation | Test on 30 noisy OHLC paths (σ=0.2% Gaussian noise). |
| 7 | OHLC Shuffle | Randomly reassign O/H/L/C roles to test price structure dependence. |
| 8 | Block Bootstrap | Resample contiguous blocks (20 bars) with replacement. |
| 9 | Deflated Sharpe Ratio | Corrects for multiple hypothesis testing (Bailey & Lopez de Prado). |
| 10 | Composite 8-dim Ranking | Sum of ranks across all 8 dimensions. Lower = better. |

### Walk-Forward Windows

```
Window 1: train [0, 35%), [embargo 5 bars], val [35%+emb, 45%), test [45%, 55%)
Window 2: train [0, 45%), [embargo 5 bars], val [45%+emb, 55%), test [55%, 65%)
Window 3: train [0, 55%), [embargo 5 bars], val [55%+emb, 65%), test [65%, 75%)
Window 4: train [0, 65%), [embargo 5 bars], val [65%+emb, 75%), test [75%, 85%)
Window 5: train [0, 75%), [embargo 5 bars], val [75%+emb, 85%), test [85%, 95%)
Window 6: train [0, 80%), [embargo 5 bars], val [80%+emb, 90%), test [90%, 100%)
```

### Execution Model

- Signal generated at **close[i]**, order filled at **open[i+1]** (next-open execution)
- Slippage: 5 basis points (0.05%)
- Commission: 15 basis points (0.15%) per trade
- These costs approximate Binance (crypto) and IBKR (stocks) retail fees

### Verdict Criteria

A strategy earns one point for each criterion met:

1. WFE > 0% (positive out-of-sample returns)
2. Generalization Gap < 5%
3. Parameter Stability > 0.5
4. Monte Carlo Score > 0.5
5. OHLC Shuffle Score > 0.3
6. Block Bootstrap Score > 0.3
7. Deflated Sharpe > 0.3
8. Cross-Asset Return > 0%

- **ROBUST**: >= 7/8 | **STRONG**: 5-6/8 | **MODERATE**: 3-4/8 | **WEAK**: < 3/8

---

## 15. Risk Disclaimer

- Past performance does NOT guarantee future results.
- All backtests use historical data and may not reflect live trading conditions.
- Despite 10 layers of anti-overfitting checks, no backtest can fully eliminate data-mining bias.
- Always use proper risk management: position sizing, stop losses, and portfolio diversification.
- Start with paper trading before deploying capital.
- Crypto markets trade 24/7 with higher volatility than equities. Adjust risk accordingly.
- This report is for educational and research purposes only, NOT investment advice.
